102152208914306009676< /user_id>
<name>Renny300<//name>< Date>
1516689627665</Date>
< Rate>
5</Rate>
< review>
This ride is very gentle and goes up to 400 ft in the air. This is a great ride for the whole family as any age can ride on the Balloon. If they are 12 or older they can ride alone, as long as the waiver is filled out by an adult. Under 12 years old a parent must accompany the child. The employees are very kind and helpful. It's tethered by a cable going up and down like an elevator. It does sway a little if there's some breezy wind passing through but it's calm. It's filled with helium, yes helium like a regular balloon would be. It's also wheelchair accessible if your wheelchair fits the gondola doors. If it doesn't fit they do have thier own wheelchair in which one can transfer into. Once in the air you can see the whole park and animals you don't normally see on the tram. Also depending on your membership level you may get a discount.<//review>

< Review>
Came here to get my first full setup of gear after borrowing and only playing once or twice a year for ~6 years.

The guys who work here were extremely nice and easy to work with. They didn't guide me too much but were there to answer questions I had and were ready to answer those questions in depth.

Overall I was very comfortable, very happy with the products I got, and ill be going back for a second gun whenever the day comes that I need a second.

The only negative was that they were out of stock on batteries and battery chargers when I got my gun so I had to go elsewhere for those. My one piece of advice when going here is to call ahead to ensure they have what you're looking for in stock - if they do then I would highly recommend going to the store as it was a good experience<//Review>

< Text>
Barber rank decreases as you move further in to the store. Barbers are extremely cautious with time as they are booked with appointments that allow them gain more revenue per cut. $20 to book an appointment for a standard taper, combover, fade, no shave, no touch on the beard. Decent price but never come here without an appointment because all of Paramount high school will be seated waiting for the next cut. Age demographic here is averaged at 18 years old. Expect a hip look with skeletal beings printed on the walls followed by a big sponsorship aimed at Suavecito. Manny with the tatted face gets down with the fades and he's fast too and he's nice. Danny with the black glove(smaller Danny) is good too. Fresh (bigger Danny, gauges, piercings) does a good job too. Look for the constant glares at the clock or at their watches. Your cut will end exactly at the half hour or on the hour. There's a scripted, "Any plans today?," which makes you feel welcomed rather than just another head on the seat. Owner does a good job at greeting customer's that walks in.<//Text>

< Name>
Elisa Lou</Name>
<Text>Probably the only food place open late on weekdays in the area. Very suitable for those late nights after coming home from a party, concert, etc. and you need a cheap little snack (or 2) to complete the evening.

I've only had the tacos here (not really a burrito person), and the quality of the meat has been consistently amazing. They are only $2.25, too. So many options to choose from - go for more of the fatty meats as they are usually most juicy. We love al pastor.

Environment and ambience is that of a typical Mexican restaurant. If you are looking for a modern, spot clean taco place, this is not going to be it. But if you want a real Mexican environment, check this place out.

There is tons of seating available and it never gets too crowded. That alone makes it better than La Taqueria (the overrated and crowded one!)

Definitely recommended.</Text><resp>None<//resp><Rating>5< /Rating>< UserId.>

I absolutely love this place; this is as legit as it gets.  The tacos are amazing, and cooked to order before your eyes.  There is a great selection of meats, including my favorite, lengua (beef tongue).  I haven't tried the cesos (brain), but it's there for you.  I also haven't tried the vegetarian burritos (including cactus), but they have an impressive selection of those as well.

Every square inch of the walls and ceiling is covered with murals.  They do have bottled beer.  Best of all, they are open until like 4am or something.  I recommend paying with cash ;)< /review>

< review>
You people are some of the most delicious in all of the mission. Especially past 2am when the hunger is strong and the need for tabletop fried intestines with radish and hotsauce is greatest! The tripas had been of varied texture, consistency, flavour, as has everything really, depending on person working the tabletop fry contraption.  This is not a bad thing. It's like being able to go to 4 different taco places all in one spot. Seating is ample, drunk super hotties stumbling around  (ok ok swaggering is better. Nay! Sauntering!!! Yes that much much better!) , whilst their dudes sit and stare at anyone who dares gaze overly intently on the skin tight white jeans or 3 size to small see through tops.... mmm mm did I say they have a really friendly and super nice staff as well as tacos? Oh. Good. It's true. Go here you plebs! Now! (Or wait till night and for tequila first)</review>

< text>
I went here with a group of friends. Most of them had tacos. Two of us had shrimp quesadillas. This place has the typical taco stand within the restaurant. You just go there and choose out your ingredients and watch your taco being made.

The quesadillas were great. They are the common quesadilla that you find here in the bay, folded almost like a buritto with no top and bottom. The ingredients were all fresh and well prepared.

This place is just a solid taqueria. You can't do wrong by going here.</text>

<user>101152759523854260389</user><user_name>Albert Chen</user_name>< time>
1385167134027< /time>
<Rate>5</Rate>< Text>
Taqueria Vallarta is my favorite place to go for tacos in SF. They have about 10 different types of meats so you can try all the weird ones. Hands down my favorite is al pastor. I can eat about 4 and they usually put a lot of meat on top with 2 tortillas per taco, so what I like to do is separate the tortillas and meat so that they are equally distributed. This gives me more room for salsa, fresh cilantro and onions. Really can't beat the price and convenience.

Last year I think the 24th street location was closed for a few months because they found out widgeons were living in the ceiling. I was severely disappointed, since 24th street is closer to me than the 16th/mission location.  One does not go to Taqueria Vallarta for cleanliness or ambience, you go there for great tacos!

I love al pastor.<//Text>

<Time>1394669169912</Time><rate>4< /rate><review>Hubs and I were on our weekly mission to dine out in SF. We wanted something quick and 'affordable'.  We both had tacos. Based on reviews I had read I was gunning for 5 tacos. Thank goodness the fella setting up the tacos misheard me and gave me 4 tacos... or maybe he did hear me and thought I was over-ordering... at any rate 4 was more than enough for me and I am a good eater.

I had:
Pollo Asado
Carne Asada
(2) Al Pastor

Hubs had:
Pollo Asado
Carne Asada
Chorizo

We both agreed hands down Pollo Asado was the best. I found this shocking, I don't usually order chicken at taquerias because I try to choose something I wouldn't make at home (we make a lot of chicken at home). Normally, Al Pastor or Carnitas are my go to. I wouldn't order the Carne Asada, Chorizo or the Al Pastor again. But I would definitely get Pollo Asado and try some other choices.

Cantaloupe Aqua Fresca was amazing (we took 3 to go), Hibiscus Aqua Fresca was good but too sweet for me to order again.

It's a cute (not cozy) interior with lots of murals to look at. Lots of tiled tables with benches.

Next time, I'm getting corn with mayo and queso and a bunch of tacos. We'll be back.<//review><pictures>None< /pictures><Response>None< /Response><gmap_id>0x808f7e4881a8f4e3:0x373f8a8597252568< /gmap_id></record>

< Text>
I bought a couple of coupons from groupon and went straight to work. I bought the tacos and burritos so thats what I'm gonna base my reviews on. Depending on certain days, the meat are really good and sometimes they can be really dry. I got a chicken burrito which was fairly good for its price which was $5.25 I think... The chicken and rice was moist and nothing taste out of the ordinary. The tacos were nice but I think they're overrated compared to the other reviews. Its just your typical taco but they have a salsa bar with a lot of different stuff such as cilantro, different salsas, toppings and etc. What I recommend is the Lengua and Cabeza because they're underrated meat. A lot of Americans never heard of these meat selections and will probably never try it because they don't want to leave their comfort zone but I love it. The meat texture is new and unique and that brings something different to the table besides the typical carne asada and pollo. I would recommend this place if you're looking for a quick cheap bite.<//Text>
